I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
task --resume-last ignores current-session scoping and can resume another Claude session's task
## Summary

`task-resume-candidate --json` is scoped to the current Claude session, but `task --resume-last` is not. In a multi-session workspace, the CLI can report that there is no resumable task for the current session and then still resume a different session's persisted Codex thread.

The same helper also lets an active task from another Claude session block `--resume-last`, even when `/codex:status` for the current session shows no running jobs.

## Reproduction

1. Start a repository with the plugin state directory available.
2. Run one successful `task` command under Claude session `sess-other` so it persists a completed task thread.
3. In a separate Claude session `sess-current`, run:
   - `node scripts/codex-companion.mjs task-resume-candidate --json`
   - `node scripts/codex-companion.mjs task --resume-last "follow up"`
4. Observe that `task-resume-candidate` reports `available: false`, but `--resume-last` still resumes the older thread from `sess-other`.
5. Alternatively, leave a `running` task owned by `sess-other` in state and run `task --resume-last` from `sess-current`.

## Expected

- Implicit resume selection should use the same current-session visibility rules as `task-resume-candidate`.
- If `CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID` is set and the current session has no resumable task, `task --resume-last` should fail with "No previous Codex task thread was found for this repository.".
- A running task from another session should not block `--resume-last` for the current session.

## Actual

- `task-resume-candidate` says there is no resumable task in the current session.
- `task --resume-last` still resumes another session's completed thread.
- A running task from another session can also block `--resume-last` with `Task ... is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.` even though `/codex:status` for the current session shows no running jobs.

## Suspected Cause

`resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(...)` scans all persisted task jobs in the workspace and only excludes the current job id. It does not apply current-session filtering before choosing a completed thread or before checking for active tasks.

## Suggested Fix

Thread the same session-aware filtering used by `task-resume-candidate` into the implicit `--resume-last` path, and only fall back to `findLatestTaskThread(...)` when there is no Claude session id in scope.


</pr_description>

   100	function normalizeRequestedModel(model) {
   101	  if (model == null) {
   102	    return null;
   103	  }
   104	  const normalized = String(model).trim();
   105	  if (!normalized) {
   106	    return null;
   107	  }
   108	  return MODEL_ALIASES.get(normalized.toLowerCase()) ?? normalized;
   109	}
   110	
   111	function normalizeReasoningEffort(effort) {
   112	  if (effort == null) {
   113	    return null;
   114	  }
   115	  const normalized = String(effort).trim().toLowerCase();
   116	  if (!normalized) {
   117	    return null;
   118	  }
   119	  if (!VALID_REASONING_EFFORTS.has(normalized)) {
   120	    throw new Error(
   121	      `Unsupported reasoning effort "${effort}". Use one of: none, minimal, low, medium, high, xhigh.`
   122	    );
   123	  }
   124	  return normalized;
   125	}
   126	
   127	function normalizeArgv(argv) {
   128	  if (argv.length === 1) {
   129	    const [raw] = argv;
   130	    if (!raw || !raw.trim()) {
   131	      return [];
   132	    }
   133	    return splitRawArgumentString(raw);
   134	  }
   135	  return argv;
   136	}
   137

   139	  return parseArgs(normalizeArgv(argv), {
   140	    ...config,

   289	function isActiveJobStatus(status) {
   290	  return status === "queued" || status === "running";
   291	}
   292	
   293	async function waitForSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, options = {}) {
   294	  const timeoutMs = Math.max(0, Number(options.timeoutMs) || DEFAULT_STATUS_WAIT_TIMEOUT_MS);
   295	  const pollIntervalMs = Math.max(100, Number(options.pollIntervalMs) || DEFAULT_STATUS_POLL_INTERVAL_MS);
   296	  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs;
   297	  let snapshot = buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   298	
   299	  while (isActiveJobStatus(snapshot.job.status) && Date.now() < deadline) {
   300	    await sleep(Math.min(pollIntervalMs, Math.max(0, deadline - Date.now())));
   301	    snapshot = buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   302	  }
   303	
   304	  return {
   305	    ...snapshot,
   306	    waitTimedOut: isActiveJobStatus(snapshot.job.status),
   307	    timeoutMs
   308	  };
   309	}
   310	
   311	async function resolveLatestTrackedTaskThread(cwd, options = {}) {
   312	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   313	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot)).filter((job) => job.id !== options.excludeJobId);
   314	  const activeTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && (job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running"));
   315	  if (activeTask) {
   316	    throw new Error(`Task ${activeTask.id} is still running. Use /codex:status before continuing it.`);
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  const trackedTask = jobs.find((job) => job.jobClass === "task" && job.status === "completed" && job.threadId);
   320	  if (trackedTask) {
   321	    return { id: trackedTask.threadId };
   322	  }
   323	
   324	  return findLatestTaskThread(workspaceRoot);
   325	}

   600	async function runForegroundCommand(job, runner, options = {}) {
   601	  const { logFile, progress } = createTrackedProgress(job, {
   602	    logFile: options.logFile,
   603	    stderr: !options.json
   604	  });
   605	  const execution = await runTrackedJob(job, () => runner(progress), { logFile });
   606	  outputResult(options.json ? execution.payload : execution.rendered, options.json);
   607	  if (execution.exitStatus !== 0) {
   608	    process.exitCode = execution.exitStatus;
   609	  }
   610	  return execution;
   611	}

   613	function spawnDetachedTaskWorker(cwd, jobId) {
   614	  const scriptPath = path.join(ROOT_DIR, "scripts", "codex-companion.mjs");
   615	  const child = spawn(process.execPath, [scriptPath, "task-worker", "--cwd", cwd, "--job-id", jobId], {

   618	    detached: true,
   619	    stdio: "ignore",
   620	    windowsHide: true
   621	  });

   704	async function handleTask(argv) {
   705	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   706	    valueOptions: ["model", "effort", "cwd", "prompt-file"],
   707	    booleanOptions: ["json", "write", "resume-last", "resume", "fresh", "background"],
   708	    aliasMap: {
   709	      m: "model"
   710	    }
   711	  });
   712	
   713	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   714	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   715	  const model = normalizeRequestedModel(options.model);
   716	  const effort = normalizeReasoningEffort(options.effort);
   717	  const prompt = readTaskPrompt(cwd, options, positionals);
   718	
   719	  const resumeLast = Boolean(options["resume-last"] || options.resume);
   720	  const fresh = Boolean(options.fresh);
   721	  if (resumeLast && fresh) {
   722	    throw new Error("Choose either --resume/--resume-last or --fresh.");
   723	  }
   724	  const write = Boolean(options.write);
   725	  const taskMetadata = buildTaskRunMetadata({
   726	    prompt,
   727	    resumeLast
   728	  });
   729	
   730	  if (options.background) {
   731	    ensureCodexReady(cwd);
   732	    requireTaskRequest(prompt, resumeLast);
   733	
   734	    const job = buildTaskJob(workspaceRoot, taskMetadata, write);
   735	    const request = buildTaskRequest({
   736	      cwd,
   737	      model,
   738	      effort,
   739	      prompt,
   740	      write,
   741	      resumeLast,
   742	      jobId: job.id
   743	    });
   744	    const { payload } = enqueueBackgroundTask(cwd, job, request);
   745	    outputCommandResult(payload, renderQueuedTaskLaunch(payload), options.json);
   746	    return;
   747	  }
   748	
   749	  const job = buildTaskJob(workspaceRoot, taskMetadata, write);
   750	  await runForegroundCommand(
   751	    job,
   752	    (progress) =>
   753	      executeTaskRun({
   754	        cwd,
   755	        model,
   756	        effort,
   757	        prompt,

   767	async function handleTaskWorker(argv) {
   768	  const { options } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   769	    valueOptions: ["cwd", "job-id"]
   770	  });
   771	
   772	  if (!options["job-id"]) {
   773	    throw new Error("Missing required --job-id for task-worker.");
   774	  }
   775	
   776	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   777	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   778	  const storedJob = readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, options["job-id"]);
   779	  if (!storedJob) {
   780	    throw new Error(`No stored job found for ${options["job-id"]}.`);
   781	  }
   782	
   783	  const request = storedJob.request;
   784	  if (!request || typeof request !== "object") {
   785	    throw new Error(`Stored job ${options["job-id"]} is missing its task request payload.`);
   786	  }
   787	
   788	  const { logFile, progress } = createTrackedProgress(
   789	    {
   790	      ...storedJob,
   791	      workspaceRoot
   792	    },
   793	    {
   794	      logFile: storedJob.logFile ?? null
   795	    }
   796	  );
   797	  await runTrackedJob(
   798	    {
   799	      ...storedJob,
   800	      workspaceRoot,
   801	      logFile
   802	    },
   803	    () =>
   804	      executeTaskRun({
   805	        ...request,
   806	        onProgress: progress
   807	      }),
   808	    { logFile }
   809	  );
   810	}
   811	
   812	async function handleStatus(argv) {
   813	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   814	    valueOptions: ["cwd", "timeout-ms", "poll-interval-ms"],
   815	    booleanOptions: ["json", "all", "wait"]
   816	  });
   817	
   818	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   819	  const reference = positionals[0] ?? "";
   820	  if (reference) {
   821	    const snapshot = options.wait
   822	      ? await waitForSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, {
   823	          timeoutMs: options["timeout-ms"],
   824	          pollIntervalMs: options["poll-interval-ms"]
   825	        })
   826	      : buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference);
   827	    outputCommandResult(snapshot, renderJobStatusReport(snapshot.job), options.json);
   828	    return;
   829	  }
   830	
   831	  if (options.wait) {
   832	    throw new Error("`status --wait` requires a job id.");
   833	  }
   834	
   835	  const report = buildStatusSnapshot(cwd, { all: options.all });
   836	  outputResult(renderStatusPayload(report, options.json), options.json);
   837	}
   838	
   839	function handleResult(argv) {
   840	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   841	    valueOptions: ["cwd"],
   842	    booleanOptions: ["json"]
   843	  });
   844	
   845	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   846	  const reference = positionals[0] ?? "";
   847	  const { workspaceRoot, job } = resolveResultJob(cwd, reference);
   848	  const storedJob = readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, job.id);
   849	  const payload = {
   850	    job,
   851	    storedJob
   852	  };
   853	
   854	  outputCommandResult(payload, renderStoredJobResult(job, storedJob), options.json);
   855	}
   856	
   857	function handleTaskResumeCandidate(argv) {
   858	  const { options } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   859	    valueOptions: ["cwd"],
   860	    booleanOptions: ["json"]
   861	  });
   862	
   863	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   864	  const workspaceRoot = resolveCommandWorkspace(options);
   865	  const sessionId = process.env[SESSION_ID_ENV] ?? null;
   866	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot));
   867	  const candidate =
   868	    jobs.find(
   869	      (job) =>
   870	        job.jobClass === "task" &&
   871	        job.threadId &&
   872	        job.status !== "queued" &&
   873	        job.status !== "running" &&
   874	        (!sessionId || job.sessionId === sessionId)
   875	    ) ?? null;
   876	
   877	  const payload = {
   878	    available: Boolean(candidate),
   879	    sessionId,
   880	    candidate:
   881	      candidate == null
   882	        ? null
   883	        : {
   884	            id: candidate.id,
   885	            status: candidate.status,
   886	            title: candidate.title ?? null,
   887	            summary: candidate.summary ?? null,
   888	            threadId: candidate.threadId,
   889	            completedAt: candidate.completedAt ?? null,
   890	            updatedAt: candidate.updatedAt ?? null
   891	          }
   892	  };
   893	
   894	  const rendered = candidate
   895	    ? `Resumable task found: ${candidate.id} (${candidate.status}).\n`
   896	    : "No resumable task found for this session.\n";
   897	  outputCommandResult(payload, rendered, options.json);
   898	}
   899	
   900	async function handleCancel(argv) {
   901	  const { options, positionals } = parseCommandInput(argv, {
   902	    valueOptions: ["cwd"],
   903	    booleanOptions: ["json"]
   904	  });
   905	
   906	  const cwd = resolveCommandCwd(options);
   907	  const reference = positionals[0] ?? "";
   908	  const { workspaceRoot, job } = resolveCancelableJob(cwd, reference);
   909	  const existing = readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, job.id) ?? {};
   910	  const threadId = existing.threadId ?? job.threadId ?? null;
   911	  const turnId = existing.turnId ?? job.turnId ?? null;
   912	
   913	  const interrupt = await interruptAppServerTurn(cwd, { threadId, turnId });
   914	  if (interrupt.attempted) {
   915	    appendLogLine(
   916	      job.logFile,
   917	      interrupt.interrupted
   918	        ? `Requested Codex turn interrupt for ${turnId} on ${threadId}.`
   919	        : `Codex turn interrupt failed${interrupt.detail ? `: ${interrupt.detail}` : "."}`
   920	    );
   921	  }
   922	
   923	  terminateProcessTree(job.pid ?? Number.NaN);
   924	  appendLogLine(job.logFile, "Cancelled by user.");
   925	
   926	  const completedAt = nowIso();
   927	  const nextJob = {
   928	    ...job,
   929	    status: "cancelled",
   930	    phase: "cancelled",
   931	    pid: null,
   932	    completedAt,
   933	    errorMessage: "Cancelled by user."
   934	  };
   935	
   936	  writeJobFile(workspaceRoot, job.id, {
   937	    ...existing,
   938	    ...nextJob,
   939	    cancelledAt: completedAt
   940	  });
   941	  upsertJob(workspaceRoot, {
   942	    id: job.id,
   943	    status: "cancelled",
   944	    phase: "cancelled",
   945	    pid: null,
   946	    errorMessage: "Cancelled by user.",
   947	    completedAt
   948	  });
   949	
   950	  const payload = {
   951	    jobId: job.id,
   952	    status: "cancelled",
   953	    title: job.title,
   954	    turnInterruptAttempted: interrupt.attempted,
   955	    turnInterrupted: interrupt.interrupted
   956	  };
   957	
   958	  outputCommandResult(payload, renderCancelReport(nextJob), options.json);
   959	}
   960	
   961	async function main() {
   962	  const [subcommand, ...argv] = process.argv.slice(2);
   963	  if (!subcommand || subcommand === "help" || subcommand === "--help") {
   964	    printUsage();
   965	    return;
   966	  }
   967	
   968	  switch (subcommand) {
   969	    case "setup":
   970	      handleSetup(argv);
   971	      break;
   972	    case "review":
   973	      await handleReview(argv);
   974	      break;
   975	    case "adversarial-review":
   976	      await handleReviewCommand(argv, {
   977	        reviewName: "Adversarial Review"
   978	      });
   979	      break;
   980	    case "task":
   981	      await handleTask(argv);
   982	      break;
   983	    case "task-worker":
   984	      await handleTaskWorker(argv);
   985	      break;
   986	    case "status":
   987	      await handleStatus(argv);
   988	      break;
   989	    case "result":
   990	      handleResult(argv);
   991	      break;
   992	    case "task-resume-candidate":
   993	      handleTaskResumeCandidate(argv);
   994	      break;
   995	    case "cancel":
   996	      await handleCancel(argv);
   997	      break;
   998	    default:
   999	      throw new Error(`Unknown subcommand: ${subcommand}`);
  1000	  }
  1001	}
  1002	
  1003	main().catch((error) => {
  1004	  const message = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
  1005	  process.stderr.write(`${message}\n`);
  1006	  process.exitCode = 1;
  1007	});

    16	      phase: typeof value.phase === "string" && value.phase.trim() ? value.phase.trim() : null,
    17	      threadId: typeof value.threadId === "string" && value.threadId.trim() ? value.threadId.trim() : null,
    18	      turnId: typeof value.turnId === "string" && value.turnId.trim() ? value.turnId.trim() : null,
    19	      stderrMessage: value.stderrMessage == null ? null : String(value.stderrMessage).trim(),
    20	      logTitle: typeof value.logTitle === "string" && value.logTitle.trim() ? value.logTitle.trim() : null,
    21	      logBody: value.logBody == null ? null : String(value.logBody).trimEnd()
    22	    };
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  return {
    26	    message: String(value ?? "").trim(),
    27	    phase: null,
    28	    threadId: null,
    29	    turnId: null,
    30	    stderrMessage: String(value ?? "").trim(),
    31	    logTitle: null,
    32	    logBody: null
    33	  };
    34	}
    35	
    36	export function appendLogLine(logFile, message) {
    37	  const normalized = String(message ?? "").trim();
    38	  if (!logFile || !normalized) {
    39	    return;
    40	  }
    41	  fs.appendFileSync(logFile, `[${nowIso()}] ${normalized}\n`, "utf8");
    42	}
    43	
    44	export function appendLogBlock(logFile, title, body) {
    45	  if (!logFile || !body) {
    46	    return;
    47	  }
    48	  fs.appendFileSync(logFile, `\n[${nowIso()}] ${title}\n${String(body).trimEnd()}\n`, "utf8");
    49	}
    50	
    51	export function createJobLogFile(workspaceRoot, jobId, title) {
    52	  const logFile = resolveJobLogFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
    53	  fs.writeFileSync(logFile, "", "utf8");
    54	  if (title) {
    55	    appendLogLine(logFile, `Starting ${title}.`);
    56	  }
    57	  return logFile;
    58	}
    59	
    60	export function createJobRecord(base, options = {}) {
    61	  const env = options.env ?? process.env;
    62	  const sessionId = env[options.sessionIdEnv ?? SESSION_ID_ENV];
    63	  return {
    64	    ...base,
    65	    createdAt: nowIso(),
    66	    ...(sessionId ? { sessionId } : {})
    67	  };
    68	}
    69	
    70	export function createJobProgressUpdater(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
    71	  let lastPhase = null;
    72	  let lastThreadId = null;
    73	  let lastTurnId = null;
    74	
    75	  return (event) => {
    76	    const normalized = normalizeProgressEvent(event);
    77	    const patch = { id: jobId };
    78	    let changed = false;
    79	
    80	    if (normalized.phase && normalized.phase !== lastPhase) {
    81	      lastPhase = normalized.phase;
    82	      patch.phase = normalized.phase;
    83	      changed = true;
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    if (normalized.threadId && normalized.threadId !== lastThreadId) {
    87	      lastThreadId = normalized.threadId;
    88	      patch.threadId = normalized.threadId;
    89	      changed = true;
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    if (normalized.turnId && normalized.turnId !== lastTurnId) {
    93	      lastTurnId = normalized.turnId;
    94	      patch.turnId = normalized.turnId;
    95	      changed = true;
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    if (!changed) {
    99	      return;
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    upsertJob(workspaceRoot, patch);
   103	
   104	    const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   105	    if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   106	      return;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    const storedJob = readJobFile(jobFile);
   110	    writeJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId, {
   111	      ...storedJob,
   112	      ...patch
   113	    });
   114	  };
   115	}
   116	
   117	export function createProgressReporter({ stderr = false, logFile = null, onEvent = null } = {}) {
   118	  if (!stderr && !logFile && !onEvent) {
   119	    return null;
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  return (eventOrMessage) => {
   123	    const event = normalizeProgressEvent(eventOrMessage);
   124	    const stderrMessage = event.stderrMessage ?? event.message;
   125	    if (stderr && stderrMessage) {
   126	      process.stderr.write(`[codex] ${stderrMessage}\n`);
   127	    }
   128	    appendLogLine(logFile, event.message);
   129	    appendLogBlock(logFile, event.logTitle, event.logBody);
   130	    onEvent?.(event);
   131	  };
   132	}
   133	
   134	function readStoredJobOrNull(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
   135	  const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   136	  if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   137	    return null;
   138	  }
   139	  return readJobFile(jobFile);
   140	}
   141	
   142	export async function runTrackedJob(job, runner, options = {}) {
   143	  const runningRecord = {
   144	    ...job,
   145	    status: "running",
   146	    startedAt: nowIso(),
   147	    phase: "starting",
   148	    pid: process.pid,
   149	    logFile: options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? null
   150	  };
   151	  writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, runningRecord);
   152	  upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, runningRecord);
   153	
   154	  try {
   155	    const execution = await runner();
   156	    const completionStatus = execution.exitStatus === 0 ? "completed" : "failed";
   157	    const completedAt = nowIso();
   158	    writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, {
   159	      ...runningRecord,
   160	      status: completionStatus,
   161	      threadId: execution.threadId ?? null,
   162	      turnId: execution.turnId ?? null,
   163	      pid: null,
   164	      phase: completionStatus === "completed" ? "done" : "failed",
   165	      completedAt,
   166	      result: execution.payload,
   167	      rendered: execution.rendered
   168	    });
   169	    upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, {
   170	      id: job.id,
   171	      status: completionStatus,
   172	      threadId: execution.threadId ?? null,
   173	      turnId: execution.turnId ?? null,
   174	      summary: execution.summary,
   175	      phase: completionStatus === "completed" ? "done" : "failed",
   176	      pid: null,
   177	      completedAt
   178	    });
   179	    appendLogBlock(options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? null, "Final output", execution.rendered);
   180	    return execution;
   181	  } catch (error) {
   182	    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);
   183	    const existing = readStoredJobOrNull(job.workspaceRoot, job.id) ?? runningRecord;
   184	    const completedAt = nowIso();
   185	    writeJobFile(job.workspaceRoot, job.id, {
   186	      ...existing,
   187	      status: "failed",
   188	      phase: "failed",
   189	      errorMessage,
   190	      pid: null,
   191	      completedAt,
   192	      logFile: options.logFile ?? job.logFile ?? existing.logFile ?? null
   193	    });
   194	    upsertJob(job.workspaceRoot, {
   195	      id: job.id,
   196	      status: "failed",
   197	      phase: "failed",
   198	      pid: null,
   199	      errorMessage,
   200	      completedAt
   201	    });
   202	    throw error;
   203	  }
   204	}

     9	const PLUGIN_DATA_ENV = "CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DATA";
    10	const FALLBACK_STATE_ROOT_DIR = path.join(os.tmpdir(), "codex-companion");

    15	function nowIso() {
    16	  return new Date().toISOString();
    17	}
    18	
    19	function defaultState() {
    20	  return {
    21	    version: STATE_VERSION,
    22	    config: {
    23	      stopReviewGate: false

    29	export function resolveStateDir(cwd) {
    30	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
    31	  let canonicalWorkspaceRoot = workspaceRoot;
    32	  try {
    33	    canonicalWorkspaceRoot = fs.realpathSync.native(workspaceRoot);
    34	  } catch {
    35	    canonicalWorkspaceRoot = workspaceRoot;
    36	  }
    37	
    38	  const slugSource = path.basename(workspaceRoot) || "workspace";
    39	  const slug = slugSource.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]+/g, "-").replace(/^-+|-+$/g, "") || "workspace";
    40	  const hash = createHash("sha256").update(canonicalWorkspaceRoot).digest("hex").slice(0, 16);
    41	  const pluginDataDir = process.env[PLUGIN_DATA_ENV];
    42	  const stateRoot = pluginDataDir ? path.join(pluginDataDir, "state") : FALLBACK_STATE_ROOT_DIR;
    43	  return path.join(stateRoot, `${slug}-${hash}`);
    44	}

    46	export function resolveStateFile(cwd) {

    58	export function loadState(cwd) {
    59	  const stateFile = resolveStateFile(cwd);
    60	  if (!fs.existsSync(stateFile)) {
    61	    return defaultState();

    63

    65	    const parsed = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(stateFile, "utf8"));

    72	      },
    73	      jobs: Array.isArray(parsed.jobs) ? parsed.jobs : []
    74	    };
    75	  } catch {
    76	    return defaultState();
    77	  }
    78	}

    80	function pruneJobs(jobs) {
    81	  return [...jobs]
    82	    .sort((left, right) => String(right.updatedAt ?? "").localeCompare(String(left.updatedAt ?? "")))
    83	    .slice(0, MAX_JOBS);
    84	}

    86	function removeFileIfExists(filePath) {
    87	  if (filePath && fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
    88	    fs.unlinkSync(filePath);
    89	  }
    90	}

    92	export function saveState(cwd, state) {
    93	  const previousJobs = loadState(cwd).jobs;
    94	  ensureStateDir(cwd);
    95	  const nextJobs = pruneJobs(state.jobs ?? []);
    96	  const nextState = {
    97	    version: STATE_VERSION,
    98	    config: {
    99	      ...defaultState().config,
   100	      ...(state.config ?? {})
   101	    },
   102	    jobs: nextJobs
   103	  };
   104	
   105	  const retainedIds = new Set(nextJobs.map((job) => job.id));
   106	  for (const job of previousJobs) {
   107	    if (retainedIds.has(job.id)) {
   108	      continue;
   109	    }
   110	    removeJobFile(resolveJobFile(cwd, job.id));
   111	    removeFileIfExists(job.logFile);
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  fs.writeFileSync(resolveStateFile(cwd), `${JSON.stringify(nextState, null, 2)}\n`, "utf8");
   115	  return nextState;
   116	}
   117	
   118	export function updateState(cwd, mutate) {
   119	  const state = loadState(cwd);
   120	  mutate(state);
   121	  return saveState(cwd, state);
   122	}

   124	export function generateJobId(prefix = "job") {
   125	  const random = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
   126	  return `${prefix}-${Date.now().toString(36)}-${random}`;
   127	}

   129	export function upsertJob(cwd, jobPatch) {
   130	  return updateState(cwd, (state) => {
   131	    const timestamp = nowIso();
   132	    const existingIndex = state.jobs.findIndex((job) => job.id === jobPatch.id);
   133	    if (existingIndex === -1) {
   134	      state.jobs.unshift({
   135	        createdAt: timestamp,
   136	        updatedAt: timestamp,
   137	        ...jobPatch
   138	      });
   139	      return;
   140	    }
   141	    state.jobs[existingIndex] = {
   142	      ...state.jobs[existingIndex],
   143	      ...jobPatch,
   144	      updatedAt: timestamp
   145	    };
   146	  });
   147	}

   157	      [key]: value
   158	    };
   159	  });

     4	import { getConfig, listJobs, readJobFile, resolveJobFile } from "./state.mjs";
     5	import { SESSION_ID_ENV } from "./tracked-jobs.mjs";
     6	import { resolveWorkspaceRoot } from "./workspace.mjs";
     7	
     8	export const DEFAULT_MAX_STATUS_JOBS = 8;
     9	export const DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES = 4;
    10	
    11	export function sortJobsNewestFirst(jobs) {
    12	  return [...jobs].sort((left, right) => String(right.updatedAt ?? "").localeCompare(String(left.updatedAt ?? "")));
    13	}
    14	
    15	function getCurrentSessionId(options = {}) {
    16	  return options.env?.[SESSION_ID_ENV] ?? process.env[SESSION_ID_ENV] ?? null;
    17	}
    18	
    19	function filterJobsForCurrentSession(jobs, options = {}) {
    20	  const sessionId = getCurrentSessionId(options);
    21	  if (!sessionId) {
    22	    return jobs;
    23	  }
    24	  return jobs.filter((job) => job.sessionId === sessionId);
    25	}
    26	
    27	function getJobTypeLabel(job) {
    28	  if (typeof job.kindLabel === "string" && job.kindLabel) {
    29	    return job.kindLabel;
    30	  }
    31	  if (job.kind === "adversarial-review") {
    32	    return "adversarial-review";
    33	  }
    34	  if (job.jobClass === "review") {
    35	    return "review";
    36	  }
    37	  if (job.jobClass === "task") {
    38	    return "rescue";
    39	  }
    40	  if (job.kind === "review") {
    41	    return "review";
    42	  }
    43	  if (job.kind === "task") {
    44	    return "rescue";
    45	  }
    46	  return "job";
    47	}
    48	
    49	function stripLogPrefix(line) {
    50	  return line.replace(/^\[[^\]]+\]\s*/, "").trim();
    51	}
    52	
    53	function isProgressBlockTitle(line) {
    54	  return (
    55	    ["Final output", "Assistant message", "Reasoning summary", "Review output"].includes(line) ||
    56	    /^Subagent .+ message$/.test(line) ||
    57	    /^Subagent .+ reasoning summary$/.test(line)
    58	  );
    59	}
    60	
    61	export function readJobProgressPreview(logFile, maxLines = DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES) {
    62	  if (!logFile || !fs.existsSync(logFile)) {
    63	    return [];
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  const lines = fs
    67	    .readFileSync(logFile, "utf8")
    68	    .split(/\r?\n/)
    69	    .map((line) => line.trimEnd())
    70	    .filter(Boolean)
    71	    .filter((line) => line.startsWith("["))
    72	    .map(stripLogPrefix)
    73	    .filter((line) => line && !isProgressBlockTitle(line));
    74	
    75	  return lines.slice(-maxLines);
    76	}
    77	
    78	function formatElapsedDuration(startValue, endValue = null) {
    79	  const start = Date.parse(startValue ?? "");
    80	  if (!Number.isFinite(start)) {
    81	    return null;
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  const end = endValue ? Date.parse(endValue) : Date.now();
    85	  if (!Number.isFinite(end) || end < start) {
    86	    return null;
    87	  }
    88	
    89	  const totalSeconds = Math.max(0, Math.round((end - start) / 1000));
    90	  const hours = Math.floor(totalSeconds / 3600);
    91	  const minutes = Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60);
    92	  const seconds = totalSeconds % 60;
    93	
    94	  if (hours > 0) {
    95	    return `${hours}h ${minutes}m`;
    96	  }
    97	  if (minutes > 0) {
    98	    return `${minutes}m ${seconds}s`;
    99	  }
   100	  return `${seconds}s`;
   101	}
   102	
   103	function looksLikeVerificationCommand(line) {
   104	  return /\b(test|tests|lint|build|typecheck|type-check|check|verify|validate|pytest|jest|vitest|cargo test|npm test|pnpm test|yarn test|go test|mvn test|gradle test|tsc|eslint|ruff)\b/i.test(
   105	    line
   106	  );
   107	}
   108	
   109	function inferLegacyJobPhase(job, progressPreview = []) {
   110	  switch (job.status) {
   111	    case "queued":
   112	      return "queued";
   113	    case "cancelled":
   114	      return "cancelled";
   115	    case "failed":
   116	      return "failed";
   117	    case "completed":
   118	      return "done";
   119	    default:
   120	      break;
   121	  }
   122	
   123	  for (let index = progressPreview.length - 1; index >= 0; index -= 1) {
   124	    const line = progressPreview[index].toLowerCase();
   125	    if (line.startsWith("starting codex") || line.startsWith("thread ready") || line.startsWith("turn started")) {
   126	      return "starting";
   127	    }
   128	    if (line.startsWith("reviewer started") || line.includes("review mode")) {
   129	      return "reviewing";
   130	    }
   131	    if (line.startsWith("searching:") || line.startsWith("calling ") || line.startsWith("running tool:")) {
   132	      return "investigating";
   133	    }
   134	    if (line.startsWith("starting collaboration tool:")) {
   135	      return "investigating";
   136	    }
   137	    if (line.startsWith("running command:")) {
   138	      return looksLikeVerificationCommand(line)
   139	        ? "verifying"
   140	        : job.jobClass === "review"
   141	          ? "reviewing"
   142	          : "investigating";
   143	    }
   144	    if (line.startsWith("command completed:")) {
   145	      return looksLikeVerificationCommand(line) ? "verifying" : "running";
   146	    }
   147	    if (line.startsWith("applying ") || line.startsWith("file changes ")) {
   148	      return "editing";
   149	    }
   150	    if (line.startsWith("turn completed")) {
   151	      return "finalizing";
   152	    }
   153	    if (line.startsWith("codex error:") || line.startsWith("failed:")) {
   154	      return "failed";
   155	    }
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  return job.jobClass === "review" ? "reviewing" : "running";
   159	}
   160	
   161	export function enrichJob(job, options = {}) {
   162	  const maxProgressLines = options.maxProgressLines ?? DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES;
   163	  const enriched = {
   164	    ...job,
   165	    kindLabel: getJobTypeLabel(job),
   166	    progressPreview:
   167	      job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running" || job.status === "failed"
   168	        ? readJobProgressPreview(job.logFile, maxProgressLines)
   169	        : [],
   170	    elapsed: formatElapsedDuration(job.startedAt ?? job.createdAt, job.completedAt ?? null),
   171	    duration:
   172	      job.status === "completed" || job.status === "failed" || job.status === "cancelled"
   173	        ? formatElapsedDuration(job.startedAt ?? job.createdAt, job.completedAt ?? job.updatedAt)
   174	        : null
   175	  };
   176	
   177	  return {
   178	    ...enriched,
   179	    phase: enriched.phase ?? inferLegacyJobPhase(enriched, enriched.progressPreview)
   180	  };
   181	}
   182	
   183	export function readStoredJob(workspaceRoot, jobId) {
   184	  const jobFile = resolveJobFile(workspaceRoot, jobId);
   185	  if (!fs.existsSync(jobFile)) {
   186	    return null;
   187	  }
   188	  return readJobFile(jobFile);
   189	}
   190	
   191	function matchJobReference(jobs, reference, predicate = () => true) {
   192	  const filtered = jobs.filter(predicate);
   193	  if (!reference) {
   194	    return filtered[0] ?? null;
   195	  }
   196	
   197	  const exact = filtered.find((job) => job.id === reference);
   198	  if (exact) {
   199	    return exact;
   200	  }
   201	
   202	  const prefixMatches = filtered.filter((job) => job.id.startsWith(reference));
   203	  if (prefixMatches.length === 1) {
   204	    return prefixMatches[0];
   205	  }
   206	  if (prefixMatches.length > 1) {
   207	    throw new Error(`Job reference "${reference}" is ambiguous. Use a longer job id.`);
   208	  }
   209	
   210	  throw new Error(`No job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to list known jobs.`);
   211	}
   212	
   213	export function buildStatusSnapshot(cwd, options = {}) {
   214	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   215	  const config = getConfig(workspaceRoot);
   216	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(filterJobsForCurrentSession(listJobs(workspaceRoot), options));
   217	  const maxJobs = options.maxJobs ?? DEFAULT_MAX_STATUS_JOBS;
   218	  const maxProgressLines = options.maxProgressLines ?? DEFAULT_MAX_PROGRESS_LINES;
   219	
   220	  const running = jobs
   221	    .filter((job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running")
   222	    .map((job) => enrichJob(job, { maxProgressLines }));
   223	
   224	  const latestFinishedRaw = jobs.find((job) => job.status !== "queued" && job.status !== "running") ?? null;
   225	  const latestFinished = latestFinishedRaw ? enrichJob(latestFinishedRaw, { maxProgressLines }) : null;
   226	
   227	  const recent = (options.all ? jobs : jobs.slice(0, maxJobs))
   228	    .filter((job) => job.status !== "queued" && job.status !== "running" && job.id !== latestFinished?.id)
   229	    .map((job) => enrichJob(job, { maxProgressLines }));
   230	
   231	  return {
   232	    workspaceRoot,
   233	    config,
   234	    sessionRuntime: getSessionRuntimeStatus(options.env),
   235	    running,
   236	    latestFinished,
   237	    recent,
   238	    needsReview: Boolean(config.stopReviewGate)
   239	  };
   240	}

   242	export function buildSingleJobSnapshot(cwd, reference, options = {}) {
   243	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   244	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot));
   245	  const selected = matchJobReference(jobs, reference);
   246	  if (!selected) {
   247	    throw new Error(`No job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to inspect known jobs.`);
   248	  }
   249	
   250	  return {
   251	    workspaceRoot,
   252	    job: enrichJob(selected, { maxProgressLines: options.maxProgressLines })
   253	  };
   254	}
   255	
   256	export function resolveResultJob(cwd, reference) {
   257	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   258	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(reference ? listJobs(workspaceRoot) : filterJobsForCurrentSession(listJobs(workspaceRoot)));
   259	  const selected = matchJobReference(
   260	    jobs,
   261	    reference,
   262	    (job) => job.status === "completed" || job.status === "failed" || job.status === "cancelled"
   263	  );
   264	
   265	  if (selected) {
   266	    return { workspaceRoot, job: selected };
   267	  }
   268	
   269	  const active = matchJobReference(jobs, reference, (job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running");
   270	  if (active) {
   271	    throw new Error(`Job ${active.id} is still ${active.status}. Check /codex:status and try again once it finishes.`);
   272	  }
   273	
   274	  if (reference) {
   275	    throw new Error(`No finished job found for "${reference}". Run /codex:status to inspect active jobs.`);
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  throw new Error("No finished Codex jobs found for this repository yet.");
   279	}
   280	
   281	export function resolveCancelableJob(cwd, reference) {
   282	  const workspaceRoot = resolveWorkspaceRoot(cwd);
   283	  const jobs = sortJobsNewestFirst(listJobs(workspaceRoot));
   284	  const activeJobs = jobs.filter((job) => job.status === "queued" || job.status === "running");
   285	
   286	  if (reference) {
   287	    const selected = matchJobReference(activeJobs, reference);
   288	    if (!selected) {
   289	      throw new Error(`No active job found for "${reference}".`);
   290	    }
   291	    return { workspaceRoot, job: selected };
   292	  }
   293	
   294	  if (activeJobs.length === 1) {
   295	    return { workspaceRoot, job: activeJobs[0] };
   296	  }
   297	  if (activeJobs.length > 1) {
   298	    throw new Error("Multiple Codex jobs are active. Pass a job id to /codex:cancel.");
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  throw new Error("No active Codex jobs to cancel.");
   302	}

   896	export async function findLatestTaskThread(cwd) {
   897	  const availability = getCodexAvailability(cwd);
   898	  if (!availability.available) {
   899	    throw new Error("Codex CLI is not installed or is missing required runtime support. Install it with `npm install -g @openai/codex`, then rerun `/codex:setup`.");
   900	  }
   901	
   902	  return withAppServer(cwd, async (client) => {
   903	    const response = await client.request("thread/list", {
   904	      cwd,
   905	      limit: 20,
   906	      sortKey: "updated_at",
   907	      sourceKinds: ["appServer"],
   908	      searchTerm: TASK_THREAD_PREFIX
   909	    });
   910	
   911	    return (
   912	      response.data.find((thread) => typeof thread.name === "string" && thread.name.startsWith(TASK_THREAD_PREFIX)) ??
   913	      null
   914	    );
   915	  });
   916	}

    99	function emitTurnCompleted(threadId, turnId, item) {
   100	  const items = Array.isArray(item) ? item : [item];
   101	  send({ method: "turn/started", params: { threadId, turn: buildTurn(turnId) } });
   102	  for (const entry of items) {
   103	    if (entry && entry.started) {
   104	      send({ method: "item/started", params: { threadId, turnId, item: entry.started } });
   105	    }
   106	    if (entry && entry.completed) {
   107	      send({ method: "item/completed", params: { threadId, turnId, item: entry.completed } });
   108	    }
   109	  }
   110	  send({ method: "turn/completed", params: { threadId, turn: buildTurn(turnId, "completed") } });
   111	}

import assert from 'node:assert/strict';
import fs from 'node:fs';
import os from 'node:os';
import path from 'node:path';
import { spawnSync } from 'node:child_process';
import { installFakeCodex, buildEnv } from '/testbed/tests/fake-codex-fixture.mjs';

const SCRIPT = '/testbed/plugins/codex/scripts/codex-companion.mjs';
const workspace = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-workspace-'));
const binDir = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-bin-'));
const pluginData = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-data-'));
installFakeCodex(binDir);
const baseEnv = { ...buildEnv(binDir), CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DATA: pluginData };
function run(args, extraEnv = {}) {
  return spawnSync(process.execPath, [SCRIPT, ...args], {
    cwd: workspace,
    env: { ...baseEnv, ...extraEnv },
    encoding: 'utf8',
  });
}

const first = run(['task', 'initial task'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-other' });
assert.equal(first.status, 0, first.stderr);
const candidate = run(['task-resume-candidate', '--json'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-current' });
assert.equal(candidate.status, 0, candidate.stderr);
console.log('candidate:', candidate.stdout.trim());
const payload = JSON.parse(candidate.stdout);
assert.equal(payload.available, false);
const resumed = run(['task', '--resume-last', 'follow up'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-current' });
console.log('resume status:', resumed.status);
console.log('resume stdout:', JSON.stringify(resumed.stdout));
console.log('resume stderr:', JSON.stringify(resumed.stderr));
if (resumed.status === 0) {
  console.error('BUG: resumed another session task');
  process.exit(2);
}
if (!resumed.stderr.includes('No previous Codex task thread was found for this repository.')) {
  console.error('Unexpected failure message');
  process.exit(3);
}
console.log('OK: did not resume other session');
EOF

import assert from 'node:assert/strict';
import fs from 'node:fs';
import os from 'node:os';
import path from 'node:path';
import { spawnSync } from 'node:child_process';
import { installFakeCodex, buildEnv } from '/testbed/tests/fake-codex-fixture.mjs';
import { resolveStateDir } from '/testbed/plugins/codex/scripts/lib/state.mjs';

const SCRIPT = '/testbed/plugins/codex/scripts/codex-companion.mjs';
const workspace = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-running-workspace-'));
const binDir = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-running-bin-'));
const pluginData = fs.mkdtempSync(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'cc-repro-running-data-'));
installFakeCodex(binDir);
const baseEnv = { ...buildEnv(binDir), CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DATA: pluginData };
function run(args, extraEnv = {}) {
  return spawnSync(process.execPath, [SCRIPT, ...args], {
    cwd: workspace,
    env: { ...baseEnv, ...extraEnv },
    encoding: 'utf8',
  });
}

const first = run(['task', 'initial task'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-current' });
assert.equal(first.status, 0, first.stderr);
const stateFile = path.join(resolveStateDir(workspace), 'state.json');
const state = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(stateFile, 'utf8'));
state.jobs.unshift({
  id: 'task-other-running',
  status: 'running',
  phase: 'running',
  jobClass: 'task',
  sessionId: 'sess-other',
  title: 'Other running task',
  summary: 'Other',
  updatedAt: '2999-01-01T00:00:00.000Z'
});
fs.writeFileSync(stateFile, JSON.stringify(state, null, 2) + '\n');

const candidate = run(['task-resume-candidate', '--json'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-current' });
assert.equal(candidate.status, 0, candidate.stderr);
console.log('candidate:', candidate.stdout.trim());
assert.equal(JSON.parse(candidate.stdout).available, true);
const resumed = run(['task', '--resume-last', 'follow up'], { CODEX_COMPANION_SESSION_ID: 'sess-current' });
console.log('resume status:', resumed.status);
console.log('resume stdout:', JSON.stringify(resumed.stdout));
console.log('resume stderr:', JSON.stringify(resumed.stderr));
assert.equal(resumed.status, 0, resumed.stderr);
assert.match(resumed.stdout, /Resumed the prior run/);
console.log('OK: other-session active task did not block current session resume');
EOF

function buildReviewJobMetadata(reviewName, target) {
  return {
    kind: reviewName === "Adversarial Review" ? "adversarial-review" : "review",
    title: reviewName === "Review" ? "Codex Review" : `Codex ${reviewName}`,
    summary: `${reviewName} ${target.label}`
  };
}

function buildTaskRunMetadata({ prompt, resumeLast = false }) {
  if (!resumeLast && String(prompt ?? "").includes(STOP_REVIEW_TASK_MARKER)) {
    return {
      title: "Codex Stop Gate Review",
      summary: "Stop-gate review of previous Claude turn"
    };
  }

  const title = resumeLast ? "Codex Resume" : "Codex Task";
  const fallbackSummary = resumeLast ? DEFAULT_CONTINUE_PROMPT : "Task";
  return {
    title,
    summary: shorten(prompt || fallbackSummary)
  };
}

function renderQueuedTaskLaunch(payload) {
  return `${payload.title} started in the background as ${payload.jobId}. Check /codex:status ${payload.jobId} for progress.\n`;
}

function getJobKindLabel(kind, jobClass) {
  if (kind === "adversarial-review") {
    return "adversarial-review";
  }
  return jobClass === "review" ? "review" : "rescue";

+function filterJobsForSessionScope(jobs, sessionId) {
+  if (!sessionId) {
+    return jobs;
+  }
+  return jobs.filter((job) => job.sessionId === sessionId);
+}
+
 function isActiveJobStatus(status) {
   return status === "queued" || status === "running";
 }
 
+function isActiveTaskJob(job) {
+  return job.jobClass === "task" && isActiveJobStatus(job.status);
+}
+
+function isResumableTaskJob(job) {
+  return job.jobClass === "task" && job.threadId && !isActiveJobStatus(job.status);
+}
